[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is classified as Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. An SSRF allows an [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause & Symptom Analysis**  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The method `parseRoot` in `ThreeDXMLParser` instantiates a bare [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXParserFactory` and calls `[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` directly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m129[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m143[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This bypasses Tika’s centralized XML security configuration, allowing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal-entity resolution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding network-based SYSTEM entities[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which leads [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto SSRF when untrusted XML-controlled URLs are fetched.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fix Approach**  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delegate all XML parsing in `parseRoot` to Tika’s secure XML utilities [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`XMLReaderUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which:  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Enforce `[0m[33mFEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m`.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Disable external-general-entities, external-parameter-entities, and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal DTD loading.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. Wrap handlers in `OfflineContentHandler` to prevent inline entity [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpansions.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the manual `SAXParserFactory` + `[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block with a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle call to `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Implementation Steps**  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. **Import Utility**  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. **Refactor `parseRoot`**  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Remove or comment out lines [0m[1;36m129[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m137[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmanual factory creation and parser [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstantiation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Inside the try-with-resources on the `InputStream`, replace  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        with  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure that `parseRoot` still declares `throws SAXException, IOException, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTikaException` so that any exceptions from `parseSAX` propagate correctly.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserving Existing Functionality**  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Handler Invocation**: `rootHandler` is passed through unchanged, so all SAX [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mevents remain delivered as before.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Parse Context & Metadata**: The same `metadata` and `context` objects are [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mforwarded, so downstream Tika logic is unaffected.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Zip Handling**: The zip-extraction logic wrapping the `InputStream` is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched; only the XML parse call is replaced.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Justification & Side-Effects**  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Security Hardened**: Leveraging `XMLReaderUtils` enforces secure XML [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeatures globally, mitigating not only SSRF but also XXE and DTD-based DoS.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Change**: A single-method swap reduces risk of regressions and keeps[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe patch focused.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Backward Compatibility**: Disallowed external entities may impact edge cases[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere remote DTDs were expected. However, Tika’s design favors offline parsing; [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate remote DTD usage is rare in 3DXML processing.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Pattern Consistency**: Other Tika parsers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., Office, PDF, HTML[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse `XMLReaderUtils.parseSAX`, so this aligns `ThreeDXMLParser` with the codebase’s[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure-parsing pattern.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No Modifications to Fuzzer, Harness, or Tests**  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged; the patch [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msolely hardens the production parser.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests and utilities are unaffected, preserving test suite integrity.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Code Range for Patch**  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parser-cad-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/threedxml/ThreeDXMLPar[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mser.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m129[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m143[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run on the `ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer` triggered a [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFuzzerSecurityIssueMedium for Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. During XML [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing, the parser attempted to connect to `jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`, indicating that [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input allowed an outbound network request. To mitigate the issue, a patch[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwas proposed in `ThreeDXMLParser.java` to replace the manual `SAXParser` [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstantiation and `[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call with Tika’s [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` helper. After applying the patch, the module failed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto compile due to a mismatched method signature: no `parseSAX` overload accepts the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfour arguments `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream, ContentHandler, Metadata, ParseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A Jazzer report flagged an SSRF attempt when parsing a 3D XML document in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ThreeDXMLParser`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace shows `Socket.connect` and then Xerces-driven XML entity [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpansion [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XMLEntityManager`, `XMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m up to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ThreeDXMLParser.parseContent`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The SSRF sanitizer detected an outbound connection to an external host derived[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom untrusted XML data.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness entry point is `ThreeDXMLParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich loads a ZIP stream and calls `parseOne`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Within `parseOne`, `XMLParser.parse` via Xerces triggers external entity [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution, leading to SSRF.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The offending code path is the manual creation of `SAXParserFactory` [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXParser` and the subsequent `[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File modified:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-cad-module/src/main/java/org/apache[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m/tika/parser/threedxml/ThreeDXMLParser.java`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Original lines [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m257[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mroot.append[0m[1;39m([0m[39mch, start, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m258[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m259[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m260[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-cad-mo[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdule/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/threedxml/ThreeDXMLParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:129[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m143[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m129[0m[39m:        SAXParserFactory factory = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m130[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m131[0m[39m:        [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m132[0m[39m:        SAXParser parser = null;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m133[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m134[0m[39m:            parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m135[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m136[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mSAXException[0m[1;39m([0m[39me[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m137[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m138[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m139[0m[39m:        RootHandler rootHandler = new [0m[1;35mRootHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m140[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m141[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m142[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m143[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Remove manual SAXParser instantiation in parseRoot:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In ThreeDXMLParser.parseRoot, delete lines that create a SAXParserFactory, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigure namespace awareness, instantiate a SAXParser, and invoke [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Specifically, remove:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     SAXParserFactory factory = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     SAXParser parser = null;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       parser = [0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       throw new [0m[1;35mSAXException[0m[1;39m([0m[39me[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace with Tika’s secure helper:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the same try-with-resources block, call the three-argument overload of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mzipFile.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrootEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, rootHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This overload automatically configures secure XML parsing [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mFEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, disables external DTDs/entities[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m via [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Import XMLReaderUtils:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add `import org.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils;` at the top of [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThreeDXMLParser.java if not already present.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Prune no-longer-used imports [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional but recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove imports of `javax.xml.parsers.SAXParserFactory`, [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`javax.xml.parsers.SAXParser`, and `javax.xml.parsers.ParserConfigurationException`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msince they are unused after the refactoring.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preserve metadata handling:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain the construction of RootHandler with `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler, metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. The [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRootHandler implements ContentHandler and writes metadata during SAX callbacks.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The metadata object remains populated via RootHandler within parseSAX.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Ensure exception compatibility:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The three-argument parseSAX throws SAXException, IOException, and [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTikaException. parseRoot already declares `throws SAXException, IOException, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTikaException`, so no signature change is needed.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Verify other usages remain intact:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The ManifestHandler invocation in processZip already uses [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, manifestHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness or test code changes are required.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Rationale:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using XMLReaderUtils.parseSAX centralizes parser configuration, applying [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity features [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., disabling external entities[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and eliminating SSRF vectors.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Dropping the metadata argument aligns with available overloads; RootHandler’s [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference to Metadata ensures metadata extraction continues uninterrupted.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing manual parser code avoids duplication and potential misconfiguration.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - parseSAX uses Tika’s default content handler wrapping; ensure that [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRootHandler’s expectations [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., character buffering[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are met. Existing tests [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould catch any regressions.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that namespace-awareness remains enabled by [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParserFactory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit calls [0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run full Tika parser test suite to confirm no unintended failures.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m10[0m[39m. References:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar secure parsing approach in other modules, e.g., in processZip’s [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mManifestHandler.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - XMLReaderUtils.getSAXParserFactory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m218[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m226[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m enforces secure processing.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
